<p>Add additional notes about how to deploy this on a live system</p>
<h2><a href="#built-with" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-built-with"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Built With</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="http://www.dropwizard.io/1.0.2/docs/" rel="nofollow">Dropwizard</a> - The web framework used</li>
<li><a href="https://maven.apache.org/" rel="nofollow">Maven</a> - Dependency Management</li>
<li><a href="https://rometools.github.io/rome/" rel="nofollow">ROME</a> - Used to generate RSS Feeds</li>
</ul>
<h2><a href="#contributing" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-contributing"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Contributing</h2>
<p>Please read <a href="https://gist.github.com/PurpleBooth/b24679402957c63ec426">CONTRIBUTING.md</a> for details on our code of conduct, and the process for submitting pull requests to us.</p>
<h2><a href="#versioning" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-versioning"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Versioning</h2>
<p>We use <a href="http://semver.org/" rel="nofollow">SemVer</a> for versioning. For the versions available, see the <a href="https://github.com/your/project/tags">tags on this repository</a>.</p>

    <div class="edit-comment-hide">
      
<table class="d-block">
  <tbody class="d-block">
    <tr class="d-block">
      <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body">
          <p>Oh nice! Thanks a lot! Finally I got around to pushing my projects to github, only to realize I didn't quite know how to structure a good readme. Now I can use this as a base and edit the relevant sections for my projects, so that the viewers can see what the repository actually is all about!</p>
<p>Some things that would be good to add (specially for hardware related projects) would be:</p>
<ul>
<li>Screenshots / Images of the set-up (for hardware include schematic / wiring diagram)</li>
<li>References (similar to acknowledgements, but may be useful to 'refer' to a particular claim/issue/reasoning.</li>
<li>Badges (which I don't know much yet about)</li>
</ul>
<p>Thanks!</p>
<p>BTW, <a href="https://guides.github.com/features/mastering-markdown/">here's a guide to markdown</a> (as listed under the comments box), the styling system used on github.</p>
      </td>
    </tr>

      <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body">
          <p>Great template!</p>
<p>Does anybody know where I can control SEO meta tags for package home page? I think that title is fetched from here in all cases :</p>
<p><a href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/4559663/33794306-629cb778-dcc9-11e7-98c0-31e2a9b2d059.png" target="_blank"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/4559663/33794306-629cb778-dcc9-11e7-98c0-31e2a9b2d059.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>But I don't know where the description is fetched? It looks like that GitHub fetch description meta tag randomly from somewhere in readme.MD, my question is if this can be controlled and defined somehow in readme.MD?<br>
I want to define what goes into meta title and meta description and see this in google results.</p>
<p><a href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/4559663/33794296-25014500-dcc9-11e7-8f53-a2b98dceeb7f.png" target="_blank"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/4559663/33794296-25014500-dcc9-11e7-8f53-a2b98dceeb7f.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
